							<p>If a function fails, this property will contain the last error as a string message, otherwise it will be undefined.</p>
						</div>
					</div>
				</section>
			</section>
			<section class="tsd-panel-group tsd-member-group ">

			<section class="tsd-panel tsd-comment">
				<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#shellscript" id="shellscript" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>ShellScript</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p><em><strong>macOS only</strong>. Requires Drafts 19 or greater.</em></p>
					<p>ShellScript objects can be used to execute Unix shell scripts.</p>
					<a href="#bash-example" id="bash-example" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Bash Example</h3>
					</a>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// define text of bash script</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> script = <span class="hljs-string">`#!/bin/bash
echo &quot;Total arguments : $#&quot;
echo &quot;1st Argument = $1&quot;
echo &quot;2nd argument = $2&quot;
`</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> runner = ShellScript.create(script);

<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (runner.execute([<span class="hljs-string">&quot;1&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;2&quot;</span>])) {
    alert(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;STDOUT: &quot;</span> + runner.standardOutput);
}
<span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
    alert(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;STDERR: &quot;</span> + runner.standardError);
}
</code></pre>
					<a href="#ruby-example" id="ruby-example" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Ruby Example</h3>
					</a>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> script = <span class="hljs-string">`#!/usr/bin/env ruby
ARGV.each do |a|
  puts &quot;Argument: #{a}&quot;
end
`</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> runner = ShellScript.create(script);

<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (runner.execute([<span class="hljs-string">&quot;1&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;2&quot;</span>])) {
    alert(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;STDOUT:\n&quot;</span> + runner.standardOutput);
}
<span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
    alert(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;STDERR:\n&quot;</span> + runner.standardError);
}
</code></pre>
					<p><strong>Note:</strong> When executed, scripts are saved to temporary files in the Drafts&#39; script directory at <code>~/Library/Application Scripts/com.agiletortoise.Drafts-OSX</code> and run. Scripts should not be written to make assumptions about their location in the file system (e.g. using relative paths). The first time a script is executed, the user will be asked to grant permissions to the script directory.</p>
				</div>
			</section>

									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

			<section class="tsd-panel tsd-comment">
				<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#medium" id="medium" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>Medium</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>Script integration with <a href="http://medium.com/">Medium.com</a>. This object handles OAuth authentication and request signing. The entire <a href="https://github.com/Medium/medium-api-docs">Medium REST API</a> can be used with the <code>request</code> method, and convenience methods are provided for common API endpoints to get user information, list publications and post.</p>
					<p>If an API calls fails, typically the result will be an <code>undefined</code> value, and the <code>lastError</code> property will contains error detail information for troubleshooting.</p>
				</div>
			</section>
			<section class="tsd-panel tsd-hierarchy">
				<h3>Hierarchy</h3>
				<ul class="tsd-hierarchy">

					</li>
				</ul>

For successful requests, the HTTPResponse object will contain an object or array or objects decoded from the JSON returned by Medium as appropriate to the request made. Refer to Medium API documentation for details about the expected parameters and responses. Drafts will handle wrapping the request in the appropriate OAuth authentication flow.</p>

			<section class="tsd-panel tsd-comment">
				<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#prompt" id="prompt" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>Prompt</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>Prompts allow the creation and display of custom dialogs to request information or confirmation from the user.</p>
					<a href="#example" id="example" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Example</h3>
					</a>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> p = Prompt.create();

p.title = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Hello&quot;</span>;
p.message = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;World!&quot;</span>;

p.addTextField(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;textFieldName&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Label&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;&quot;</span>);

p.addDatePicker(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;myDate&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Start date&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">Date</span>(), {
  <span class="hljs-string">&quot;mode&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;date&quot;</span>
});
p.addButton(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;First&quot;</span>);
p.addButton(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Second&quot;</span>);

<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> didSelect = p.show();

<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> textFieldContents = p.fieldValues[<span class="hljs-string">&quot;textFieldName&quot;</span>];
<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> startDate = p.fieldValues[<span class="hljs-string">&quot;myDate&quot;</span>];

<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (p.buttonPressed == <span class="hljs-string">&quot;First&quot;</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// do something</span>
}
</code></pre>
				</div>

				<section class="tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-kind-property tsd-parent-kind-class">
					<a name="iscancellable" class="tsd-anchor"></a>
					<h3>is<wbr>Cancellable</h3>
					<div class="tsd-signature tsd-kind-icon">is<wbr>Cancellable<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span> <span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span></div>
					<aside class="tsd-sources">
						<ul>
							<li>Defined in <a href="https://github.com/agiletortoise/drafts-script-reference/blob/bb281e8/src/Prompt.d.ts#L63">Prompt.d.ts:63</a></li>
						</ul>
					</aside>
					<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
						<div class="lead">
							<p>If true, a &quot;Cancel&quot; button will be included in the dialog. Defaults to <code>true</code>. If the user selects the cancel button, the <code>show()</code> method will return <code>false</code>. If <code>false</code>, no cancel button will be displayed and the user must select one of the button name options.</p>
						</div>
					</div>
				</section>
				<section class="tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-kind-property tsd-parent-kind-class">

							<li>Defined in <a href="https://github.com/agiletortoise/drafts-script-reference/blob/bb281e8/src/Prompt.d.ts#L57">Prompt.d.ts:57</a></li>
						</ul>
					</aside>
					<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
						<div class="lead">
							<p>A longer message explaining the purpose of the dialog, if needed.</p>
						</div>
					</div>
				</section>

					<div class="tsd-signature tsd-kind-icon">button<wbr>Pressed<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span> <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></div>
					<aside class="tsd-sources">
						<ul>
							<li>Defined in <a href="https://github.com/agiletortoise/drafts-script-reference/blob/bb281e8/src/Prompt.d.ts#L75">Prompt.d.ts:75</a></li>
						</ul>
					</aside>
					<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
						<div class="lead">
							<p>After the <code>show()</code> method is called, this property will contain the name of the button selected by the user.</p>
						</div>
					</div>
				</section>
				<section class="tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-kind-property tsd-parent-kind-class">
					<a name="fieldvalues" class="tsd-anchor"></a>
					<h3>field<wbr>Values</h3>
					<div class="tsd-signature tsd-kind-icon">field<wbr>Values<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">:</span> <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{}</span></div>
					<aside class="tsd-sources">
						<ul>
							<li>Defined in <a href="https://github.com/agiletortoise/drafts-script-reference/blob/bb281e8/src/Prompt.d.ts#L69">Prompt.d.ts:69</a></li>
						</ul>
					</aside>
					<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
						<div class="lead">
							<p>After the <code>show()</code> method is called, this property will contain values from any fields added to the prompt. The dictionary keys will be the names of the fields as passed in when they were created, and the value will be the current contents of that field. They type of data depends on the type of field.</p>
						</div>
					</div>

							</li>

			<section class="tsd-panel-group tsd-member-group ">
				<h2>Field Methods</h2>
				<section class="tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class">
					<a name="addbutton" class="tsd-anchor"></a>
					<h3>add<wbr>Button</h3>
					<ul class="tsd-signatures tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class">
						<li class="tsd-signature tsd-kind-icon">add<wbr>Button<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">(</span>name<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span>, value<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">object</span>, isDefault<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">)</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">void</span></li>
					</ul>
					<ul class="tsd-descriptions">
						<li class="tsd-description">
							<aside class="tsd-sources">
								<ul>
									<li>Defined in <a href="https://github.com/agiletortoise/drafts-script-reference/blob/bb281e8/src/Prompt.d.ts#L221">Prompt.d.ts:221</a></li>
								</ul>
							</aside>
							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Add a button to the array of buttons to be displayed. All buttons should be created before calling <code>show()</code>.</p>
								</div>
							</div>
							<h4 class="tsd-parameters-title">Parameters</h4>
							<ul class="tsd-parameters">
								<li>
									<h5>name: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5><span class="tsd-flag ts-flagOptional">Optional</span> value: <span class="tsd-signature-type">object</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>only needed to associate a different value than will be displayed in the button. For example, if you call <code>prompt.addButton(&quot;First Button&quot;, 1)</code>, after calling <code>prompt.show()</code> if that button is pressed, the <code>prompt.buttonPressed</code> will contain the number value <code>1</code>.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5><span class="tsd-flag ts-flagOptional">Optional</span> isDefault: <span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>used to specify a single button which will be pinned to the bottom of the prompt and respond to <code>cmd + return</code> as the default button. If only one button is added to a prompt, it is assumed to be the default.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
							</ul>
							<h4 class="tsd-returns-title">Returns <span class="tsd-signature-type">void</span></h4>
						</li>
					</ul>
				</section>
				<section class="tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class">
					<a name="adddatepicker" class="tsd-anchor"></a>
					<h3>add<wbr>Date<wbr>Picker</h3>
					<ul class="tsd-signatures tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class">
						<li class="tsd-signature tsd-kind-icon">add<wbr>Date<wbr>Picker<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">(</span>name<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span>, label<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span>, initialDate<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">Date</span>, options<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{ </span>maximumDate<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">Date</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">; </span>minimumDate<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">Date</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">; </span>minuteInterval<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">number</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">; </span>mode<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">"date"</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol"> | </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">"time"</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol"> | </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">"dateAndTime"</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol"> }</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">)</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">void</span></li>
					</ul>
					<ul class="tsd-descriptions">
						<li class="tsd-description">
							<aside class="tsd-sources">
								<ul>
									<li>Defined in <a href="https://github.com/agiletortoise/drafts-script-reference/blob/bb281e8/src/Prompt.d.ts#L170">Prompt.d.ts:170</a></li>
								</ul>
							</aside>
							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Add a date and/or time picker to the prompt, with the arguments as below. The <code>fieldValues</code> entry for this will be a date object.</p>
								</div>
							</div>
							<h4 class="tsd-parameters-title">Parameters</h4>
							<ul class="tsd-parameters">
								<li>
									<h5>name: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>Identifier for the field. This will be used as the key in the <code>fieldValues</code> dictionary to access the contents of the field after calling <code>show()</code>.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5>label: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>User-friendly text label to place next to the field.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5>initialDate: <span class="tsd-signature-type">Date</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>The initial date to selected for the field. Minimum and maximum values should be defined in options.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>

					<ul class="tsd-signatures tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class">
						<li class="tsd-signature tsd-kind-icon">add<wbr>Picker<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">(</span>name<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span>, label<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span>, columns<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[]</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[]</span>, selectedRows<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">number</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[]</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">)</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">void</span></li>

								</ul>
							</aside>
							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Add a picker to the prompt, with the arguments as below. Picker can contain multiple rows. The <code>fieldValues</code> entry for this will be a array of selected index values object.</p>
								</div>
							</div>
							<h4 class="tsd-parameters-title">Parameters</h4>
							<ul class="tsd-parameters">
								<li>
									<h5>name: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>Identifier for the field. This will be used as the key in the <code>fieldValues</code> dictionary to access the contents of the field after calling <code>show()</code>.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5>label: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>User-friendly text label to place next to the field.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5>columns: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[]</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[]</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>The values to display in the picker. Should be an array containing arrays of string values, each sub-array representing a column in the picker. Example two column picker: <code>[[&quot;Item 1&quot;, &quot;Item 2&quot;],[&quot;Column 2 Item 1&quot;, &quot;Column 2 Item 2&quot;|&quot;Item 1&quot;, &quot;Item 2&quot;],[&quot;Column 2 Item 1&quot;, &quot;Column 2 Item 2&quot;]]</code></p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5>selectedRows: <span class="tsd-signature-type">number</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[]</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>Array of zero-based index values to set the initial selected row in each column.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
							</ul>
							<h4 class="tsd-returns-title">Returns <span class="tsd-signature-type">void</span></h4>
						</li>
					</ul>
				</section>

					<ul class="tsd-signatures tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class">

							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

									<p>Add a select control. Returns an array of string values in <code>fieldValues</code>.</p>
								</div>
							</div>
							<h4 class="tsd-parameters-title">Parameters</h4>
							<ul class="tsd-parameters">
								<li>
									<h5>name: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>Identifier for the field. This will be used as the key in the <code>fieldValues</code> dictionary to access the contents of the field after calling <code>show()</code>.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5>label: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">

									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5>values: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[]</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>The array of string values that will be available to select.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5>selectedValues: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[]</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>Array of string values that should be initially selected when the prompt is displayed. All values in this array should match values in the <code>values</code> array.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5>allowMultiple: <span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>If <code>false</code>, selecting a value will deselect all other values. If <code>true</code>, the user may select multiple items.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
							</ul>

						</li>

				<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#box" id="box" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>Box</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>Box objects can be used to work with files in a Box.com account.</p>
					<a href="#examples" id="examples" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Examples</h3>
					</a>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// create Box object</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> drive = Box.create();

<span class="hljs-comment">// setup variables</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> path = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;/test/file.txt&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> content = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;text to place in file&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// write to file on Box</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> success = drive.write(path, content, <span class="hljs-literal">false</span>);

<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (success) { <span class="hljs-comment">// write worked!</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> driveContent = drive.read(path);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (driveContent) { <span class="hljs-comment">// read worked!</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (driveContent == content) {
      alert(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;File contents match!&quot;</span>);
    }
    <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
      <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;File did not match&quot;</span>);
      context.fail();
    }
  }
  <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> { <span class="hljs-comment">// read failed, log error</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(drive.lastError);
    context.fail();
  }
}
<span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> { <span class="hljs-comment">// write failed, log error</span>
  <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(drive.lastError);
  context.fail();
}
</code></pre>
				</div>

							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Reads the contents of the file at the path as a string. Returns <code>undefined</code> value if the file does not exist or could not be read. Paths should begin with a <code>/</code> and be relative to the root directory of your Box.com account.</p>
								</div>
							</div>
							<h4 class="tsd-parameters-title">Parameters</h4>
							<ul class="tsd-parameters">
								<li>
									<h5>path: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
									</div>
								</li>
							</ul>
							<h4 class="tsd-returns-title">Returns <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h4>
						</li>
					</ul>
				</section>
				<section class="tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class">
					<a name="write" class="tsd-anchor"></a>
					<h3>write</h3>
					<ul class="tsd-signatures tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class">
						<li class="tsd-signature tsd-kind-icon">write<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">(</span>path<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span>, content<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span>, overwrite<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">)</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span></li>
					</ul>
					<ul class="tsd-descriptions">
						<li class="tsd-description">
							<aside class="tsd-sources">
								<ul>
									<li>Defined in <a href="https://github.com/agiletortoise/drafts-script-reference/blob/bb281e8/src/Box.d.ts#L56">Box.d.ts:56</a></li>
								</ul>
							</aside>
							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Write the contents of the file at the path. Returns true if successful, false if the file could not be written successfully. This will override existing files!</p>
								</div>
							</div>
							<h4 class="tsd-parameters-title">Parameters</h4>
							<ul class="tsd-parameters">
								<li>
									<h5>path: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>Paths should begin with a <code>/</code> and be relative to the root directory of your Box</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5>content: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>Text to place in the file.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5><span class="tsd-flag ts-flagOptional">Optional</span> overwrite: <span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>If false, an existing file will not be overwritten.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
							</ul>
							<h4 class="tsd-returns-title">Returns <span class="tsd-signature-type">boolean</span></h4>
						</li>
					</ul>
				</section>
				<section class="tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class tsd-is-static">

								</ul>
							</aside>
							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Creates a new Box object. Identifier is a optional string value used to identify a Box.com account. Typically this can be omitted if you only work with one Box.com account in Drafts.</p>

									<li data-value="private" class="selected">All</li>
								</ul>
							</div>

	<div class="tsd-page-title">

			<h1>Class XMLRPC</h1>
		</div>
	</div>
</header>
<div class="container container-main">
	<div class="row">
		<div class="col-8 col-content">
			<section class="tsd-panel tsd-comment">
				<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#xmlrpc" id="xmlrpc" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>XMLRPC</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>The XMLRPC object is a convenience method to provide an easy way to <a href="http://xmlrpc.scripting.com/">XML-RPC</a> web services. The request function takes care of converting native Javascript objects and values to the XML parameters required for the XML-RPC interface, and converts the XML responses returned to Javascript objects.</p>
					<p>It will also return faults parsed to error messages in the response if necessary.</p>
					<p>This object is suitable for communication with a number of popular XML-RPC interfaces, including the <a href="http://xmlrpc.scripting.com/metaWeblogApi.html">MetaWeblog API</a>. WordPress also offers its own XML-RPC interface, which can be used via this object, or the convenience wrapper <code>WordPress</code> object.</p>
					<a href="#example-xml-rpc-call" id="example-xml-rpc-call" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Example: XML-RPC call</h3>
					</a>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// DEMO of XML-RPC</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Calls example method on http://xml-rpc.net/index.html</span>

<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> url = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;http://www.cookcomputing.com/xmlrpcsamples/RPC2.ashx&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> methodName = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;examples.getStateName&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> params = [<span class="hljs-number">20</span>];

<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> response = XMLRPC.request(url, methodName, params);

<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (response.success) {
    alert(<span class="hljs-built_in">JSON</span>.stringify(response.params));
}
<span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
    alert(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Fault: &quot;</span> + response.faultCode + <span class="hljs-string">&quot;, &quot;</span> + response.error);
    context.fail();
}
</code></pre>
				</div>
			</section>
			<section class="tsd-panel tsd-hierarchy">
				<h3>Hierarchy</h3>
				<ul class="tsd-hierarchy">
					<li>
						<span class="target">XMLRPC</span>
					</li>
				</ul>
			</section>
			<section class="tsd-panel-group tsd-index-group">
				<h2>Index</h2>

							</ul>

					</div>
				</section>
			</section>

				<h2>Methods</h2>
				<section class="tsd-panel tsd-member tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class tsd-is-static">
					<a name="request" class="tsd-anchor"></a>
					<h3><span class="tsd-flag ts-flagStatic">Static</span> request</h3>
					<ul class="tsd-signatures tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class tsd-is-static">
						<li class="tsd-signature tsd-kind-icon">request<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">(</span>url<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span>, methodName<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span>, params<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">any</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[]</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">)</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><a href="xmlrpcresponse.html" class="tsd-signature-type">XMLRPCResponse</a></li>
					</ul>
					<ul class="tsd-descriptions">
						<li class="tsd-description">
							<aside class="tsd-sources">
								<ul>
									<li>Defined in <a href="https://github.com/agiletortoise/drafts-script-reference/blob/bb281e8/src/XML-RPC.d.ts#L39">XML-RPC.d.ts:39</a></li>
								</ul>
							</aside>
							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Make an XML-RPC request.</p>
								</div>
							</div>
							<h4 class="tsd-parameters-title">Parameters</h4>
							<ul class="tsd-parameters">
								<li>
									<h5>url: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>The full URL of the XML-RPC host endpoint being called.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5>methodName: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>Name of the method to call. Supported values are specific to the services provided by the host.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
								<li>
									<h5>params: <span class="tsd-signature-type">any</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[]</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>The parameters to pass to the request. This should be an array of values, in the proper order, as specified by the documentation of the host being called. This array will be encoded into XML-RPC parameters in XML format by the method - only raw javascript values should be provided.</p>
									</div>
								</li>
							</ul>
							<h4 class="tsd-returns-title">Returns <a href="xmlrpcresponse.html" class="tsd-signature-type">XMLRPCResponse</a></h4>

			<section class="tsd-panel tsd-comment">
				<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#script" id="script" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>Script</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>When running a <a href="https://docs.getdrafts.com/docs/actions/steps/advanced.html#script">Script action step</a>, a single <code>script</code> object will be in context to reference the currently running script.</p>
					<a href="#example" id="example" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Example</h3>
					</a>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">sleep</span>(<span class="hljs-params">milliseconds</span>) </span>{
  <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> start = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">Date</span>().getTime();
  <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="hljs-number">1e7</span>; i++) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> ((<span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">Date</span>().getTime() - start) &gt; milliseconds){
      <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    }
  }
}
<span class="hljs-keyword">async</span> <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">f</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) </span>{
  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> promise = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">Promise</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">resolve, reject</span>) =&gt;</span> {
    sleep(<span class="hljs-number">1000</span>);
    resolve(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;done!&quot;</span>)
  });
  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> result = <span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> promise; <span class="hljs-comment">// wait until the promise resolves (*)</span>
  alert(result); <span class="hljs-comment">// &quot;done!&quot;</span>
  script.complete();
}
f();
</code></pre>
				</div>
			</section>

					<a name="complete" class="tsd-anchor"></a>
					<h3>complete</h3>
					<ul class="tsd-signatures tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class">
						<li class="tsd-signature tsd-kind-icon">complete<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">(</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">)</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">any</span></li>
					</ul>
					<ul class="tsd-descriptions">
						<li class="tsd-description">
							<aside class="tsd-sources">
								<ul>
									<li>Defined in <a href="https://github.com/agiletortoise/drafts-script-reference/blob/bb281e8/src/Script.d.ts#L32">Script.d.ts:32</a></li>
								</ul>
							</aside>
							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Inform Drafts the current script has completed execution. Used in combination with the &quot;Allow asynchronous execution&quot; option of the Script step type. If your script step has the asynchronous option enabled, you <em>must</em> call <code>script.complete()</code> to indicate completion or the script will timeout and fail.</p>
								</div>
							</div>
							<h4 class="tsd-returns-title">Returns <span class="tsd-signature-type">any</span></h4>
						</li>
					</ul>

<div class="container container-main">
	<div class="row">
		<div class="col-8 col-content">
			<section class="tsd-panel tsd-comment">
				<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#todoist" id="todoist" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>Todoist</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>Script integration with <a href="http://todoist.com/">Todoist</a>. This object handles OAuth authentication and request signing. The entire <a href="https://developer.todoist.com/rest/v1/">Todoist REST API</a> can be used with the request method, and convenience methods are provided for common API endpoints to manage tasks, projects, comments and labels.</p>
					<p>The <code>quickAdd</code> method is mostly likely what you are looking for to create tasks as it supports the shorthand the task entry box in Todoist supports to parse projects, etc.</p>
					<p>Other methods are direct mappings of the REST API calls provided by Todoist. Most take an <code>options</code> parameter which is a javascript object containing the parameters to be passed to the API, and and the method decodes the JSON response from Todoist and returns it as a Javascript object (or array of objects) with the values as specified in the Todoist API docs.</p>
					<p>If an API calls fails, typically the result will be an <code>undefined</code> value, and the <code>lastError</code> property will contains error detail information for troubleshooting.</p>
					<a href="#example" id="example" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Example</h3>
					</a>
					<p>See <a href="https://actions.getdrafts.com/g/1L3">Examples-Todoist</a> action group in the <a href="https://actions.getdrafts.com/">Action Directory</a>.</p>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// create Todoist object</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> todoist = Todoist.create();
<span class="hljs-comment">// create task in inbox</span>
todoist.createTask({
  <span class="hljs-string">&quot;content&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;My Task Name&quot;</span>,
  <span class="hljs-string">&quot;due_string&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Next wednesday&quot;</span>
});
</code></pre>
				</div>
			</section>
			<section class="tsd-panel tsd-hierarchy">
				<h3>Hierarchy</h3>
				<ul class="tsd-hierarchy">

				</ul>
			</section>

					<h3>request</h3>
					<ul class="tsd-signatures tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class">
						<li class="tsd-signature tsd-kind-icon">request<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">(</span>settings<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{ </span>data<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">; </span>headers<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">; </span>method<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">; </span>parameters<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">; </span>url<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol"> }</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">)</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><a href="httpresponse.html" class="tsd-signature-type">HTTPResponse</a></li>
					</ul>
					<ul class="tsd-descriptions">
						<li class="tsd-description">
							<aside class="tsd-sources">
								<ul>
									<li>Defined in <a href="https://github.com/agiletortoise/drafts-script-reference/blob/bb281e8/src/Todoist.d.ts#L177">Todoist.d.ts:177</a></li>
								</ul>
							</aside>
							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Execute a request against the Todoist API. For successful requests, the HTTPResponse object will contain an object or array or objects decoded from the JSON returned by Todoist as appropriate to the request made. Refer to Todoist’s API documentation for details about the expected parameters and responses. Drafts will handle wrapping the request in the appropriate OAuth authentication flow.</p>
								</div>
							</div>
							<h4 class="tsd-parameters-title">Parameters</h4>
							<ul class="tsd-parameters">
								<li>
									<h5>settings: <span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{ </span>data<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">; </span>headers<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">; </span>method<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">; </span>parameters<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{}</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">; </span>url<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol"> }</span></h5>
									<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
										<p>an object configuring the request.</p>
									</div>
									<ul class="tsd-parameters">
										<li class="tsd-parameter">
											<h5><span class="tsd-flag ts-flagOptional">Optional</span> data<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{}</span></h5>
											<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
												<div class="lead">
													<p>A JavaScript object containing data to be encoded into the HTTP body of the request.</p>
												</div>
											</div>
											<ul class="tsd-parameters">
												<li class="tsd-parameter-index-signature">
													<h5><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[</span>x: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">]: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
												</li>
											</ul>
										</li>
										<li class="tsd-parameter">
											<h5><span class="tsd-flag ts-flagOptional">Optional</span> headers<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{}</span></h5>
											<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
												<div class="lead">
													<p>An object contain key-values to be added as custom headers in the request. There is no need to provide authorization headers, Drafts will add those.</p>
												</div>
											</div>
											<ul class="tsd-parameters">
												<li class="tsd-parameter-index-signature">
													<h5><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[</span>x: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">]: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
												</li>
											</ul>
										</li>
										<li class="tsd-parameter">
											<h5>method<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
											<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
												<div class="lead">
													<p>The HTTP method, like &quot;GET&quot;, &quot;POST&quot;, etc.</p>
												</div>
											</div>
										</li>
										<li class="tsd-parameter">
											<h5><span class="tsd-flag ts-flagOptional">Optional</span> parameters<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">?: </span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">{}</span></h5>
											<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
												<div class="lead">
													<p>An object containing key-values to be added to the request as URL parameters.</p>
												</div>
											</div>
											<ul class="tsd-parameters">
												<li class="tsd-parameter-index-signature">
													<h5><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">[</span>x: <span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span><span class="tsd-signature-symbol">]: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
												</li>
											</ul>
										</li>
										<li class="tsd-parameter">
											<h5>url<span class="tsd-signature-symbol">: </span><span class="tsd-signature-type">string</span></h5>
											<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
												<div class="lead">
													<p>The full URL to the endpoint in the <a href="https://developer.todoist.com/rest/v1/">Todoist REST API</a>.</p>
												</div>
											</div>
										</li>
									</ul>
								</li>
							</ul>

					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#alarm" id="alarm" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>Alarm</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>Alarms are alerts which can be attached to <a href="reminder.html">Reminder</a> and <a href="event.html">Event</a> objects.</p>
					<a href="#examples" id="examples" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Examples</h3>
					</a>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> list = ReminderList.findOrCreate(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Errands&quot;</span>);
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> reminder = list.createReminder();
reminder.title = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Get more paper towels&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> alarm = Alarm.alarmWithDate((<span class="hljs-number">3</span>).days().fromNow());
reminder.addAlarm(alarm);
reminder.update();
</code></pre>
				</div>
			</section>

					<ul class="tsd-signatures tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class tsd-is-static">

								</ul>
							</aside>
							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Alarm set to remind at a specific number of seconds relative to the start date of the event. Note that alarms created with this methods are only supported on <a href="event.html">Event</a> objects, not <a href="reminder.html">Reminder</a> objects.</p>

					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#reminderlist" id="reminderlist" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>ReminderList</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>ReminderList objects are used to manipulate and create lists in the built-in Reminders app.</p>
					<a href="#examples" id="examples" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Examples</h3>
					</a>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> list = ReminderList.findOrCreate(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Groceries&quot;</span>);
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> reminder = list.createReminder();
reminder.title = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Bananas&quot;</span>;
reminder.notes = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Get slightly green ones.&quot;</span>
reminder.update();
</code></pre>
				</div>

							<h1>Reminder</h1>
						</a>

									<li>Defined in <a href="https://github.com/agiletortoise/drafts-script-reference/blob/bb281e8/src/Reminder.d.ts#L89">Reminder.d.ts:89</a></li>
								</ul>
							</aside>
							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Add an alarm object to the reminder. Be sure to <code>update()</code> to save after adding alarms. Return <code>true</code> if the alarm was successfully added. Note that reminders only support alarms created with the <code>Alarm.alarmWithDate</code> method.</p>
								</div>
							</div>

		<div class="col-8 col-content">
			<section class="tsd-panel tsd-comment">
				<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#microsofttodo" id="microsofttodo" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>MicrosoftToDo</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>Script integration with <a href="http://todo.microsoft.com/">Microsoft To Do</a>. This object handles OAuth authentication and request signing. The entire <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/api/resources/todo-overview?view=graph-rest-1.0">Microsoft To Do Graph API</a> can be used with the <code>request</code> method, and convenience methods are provided for common API endpoints to manage tasks and lists.</p>
					<p>Working with the return values and parameters for these methods requires an understanding of the JSON objects created and returned by the API, so refer to type specifications in the <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/api/resources/todo-overview?view=graph-rest-1.0">API Reference</a> for details on values supported in task and lists. Specifically, review the supported properties of the <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/api/resources/todotask?view=graph-rest-1.0">Task</a> and <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/api/resources/todotasklist?view=graph-rest-1.0">TaskList</a> objects to understand the values included in fetched objects, and to make modifications.</p>
					<p>If an API calls fails, typically the result will be an <code>undefined</code> value, and the <code>lastError</code> property will contains error detail information for troubleshooting.</p>
					<a href="#example" id="example" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Example</h3>
					</a>
					<p>See <a href="https://actions.getdrafts.com/g/1m3">Examples-Microsoft To Do</a> action group in the <a href="https://actions.getdrafts.com/">Drafts Directory</a>. It contains several example scripted actions.</p>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// create MicrosoftToDo object</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> todo = MicrosoftToDo.create();
<span class="hljs-comment">// create task in &quot;Test&quot; list</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> list = todo.findList(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Test&quot;</span>);
<span class="hljs-comment">// create task object, more properties available, see API docs</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> task = {
<span class="hljs-string">&quot;title&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-string">`Task Title`</span>,
<span class="hljs-string">&quot;importance&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;high&quot;</span>,
<span class="hljs-string">&quot;body&quot;</span>: {
<span class="hljs-string">&quot;content&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Notes for the task&quot;</span>,
<span class="hljs-string">&quot;contentType&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;text&quot;</span>
};
<span class="hljs-string">&quot;dueDateTime&quot;</span>: {
<span class="hljs-string">&quot;dateTime&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">Date</span>.today().addDays(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>).toISOString(),
<span class="hljs-string">&quot;timeZone&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;UTC&quot;</span>
}
};
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> t = todo.createTask(list, task);
</code></pre>
				</div>
			</section>

					<ul class="tsd-signatures tsd-kind-method tsd-parent-kind-class">

							<aside class="tsd-sources">
								<ul>
									<li>Defined in <a href="https://github.com/agiletortoise/drafts-script-reference/blob/bb281e8/src/MicrosoftToDo.d.ts#L105">MicrosoftToDo.d.ts:105</a></li>
								</ul>
							</aside>
							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Create new linked resource for a task. A linked resource is a reference to content in an external system, such as a link back to a draft. <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/api/resources/linkedresource?view=graph-rest-1.0">API documentation</a></p>
								</div>
							</div>
							<h4 class="tsd-parameters-title">Parameters</h4>

								</ul>
							</aside>
							<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
								<div class="lead">
									<p>Execute a request against the <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/api/resources/todo-overview?view=graph-rest-1.0">Microsoft To Do API</a>. For successful requests, the HTTPResponse object will contain an object or array or objects decoded from the JSON returned by the API as appropriate to the request made. Refer to API documentation for details about the expected parameters and responses. Drafts will handle wrapping the request in the appropriate OAuth authentication flow.
									Requests should only be made to endpoints in the Microsoft Graph API which require the <code>Task.ReadWrite</code> authentication scope.</p>
								</div>

<div class="container container-main">
	<div class="row">
		<div class="col-8 col-content">
			<section class="tsd-panel tsd-comment">
				<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#wordpress" id="wordpress" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>WordPress</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>Script integration with WordPress sites via the <a href="https://codex.wordpress.org/XML-RPC_WordPress_API">WordPress XML-RPC API</a>. Currently this object has one runMethod function which can be used to call any method available in the XML-RPC interface.</p>
					<p>The WordPress API offers access to a wide variety of functions, including posting, but also retrieving information about categories and tags, or reading posts contents.</p>
					<p>Drafts <code>WordPress</code> object simplifies working with the XML-RPC interface by accepting input parameters as Javascript objects and converting them to the require XML to make requests of the WordPress site. Similarly, it converts to XML returned by WordPress to Javascript objects. Otherwise it is an exact passthrough, so the <a href="https://codex.wordpress.org/XML-RPC_WordPress_API">WordPress API reference</a> should be used to determine method names (e.g. <code>wp.newPost</code>, <code>wp.getTaxonomies</code>) available, the appropriate parameters to send.</p>
					<p>The WordPress XML-RPC API authenticates via username and password, so it is highly recommended you interact only over HTTPS secure connections, and use <code>Credential</code> objects to store host/username/password values, rather than hard-coding them in actions.</p>
					<a href="#example" id="example" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Example</h3>
					</a>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// setup values to use in post</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> title = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Title of Post&quot;</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> body = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Body of Post&quot;</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// create credentials for site</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> cred = Credential.createWithHostUsernamePassword(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;WordPress&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;WordPress  * credentials. Include full URL (with http://) of the home page of your WordPress  * site in the host field.&quot;</span>);
cred.authorize();

<span class="hljs-comment">// create WordPress object and make request</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> wp = WordPress.create(cred.getValue(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;host&quot;</span>), <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;&quot;</span>);
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> method = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;wp.newPost&quot;</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> params = [
    <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// blog_id, in most cases just use 1</span>
    cred.getValue(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;username&quot;</span>),
    cred.getValue(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;password&quot;</span>),
    {
        <span class="hljs-string">&quot;post_title&quot;</span>: title,
        <span class="hljs-string">&quot;post_content&quot;</span>: body,
        <span class="hljs-string">&quot;post_status&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;draft&quot;</span>,
        <span class="hljs-string">&quot;terms_names&quot;</span> : { <span class="hljs-comment">// assign categories and tags</span>
            <span class="hljs-string">&quot;category&quot;</span> : [<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Cat1&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;BAD&quot;</span>],
            <span class="hljs-string">&quot;post_tag&quot;</span> : [<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Test1&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;NOT-TAG&quot;</span>]
        }
    }
];

<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> response = wp.runMethod(method, params);
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (response.success) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> params = response.params;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Create WordPress post id: &quot;</span> + params[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]);
}
<span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
    <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;HTTP Status: &quot;</span> + response.statusCode);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Fault: &quot;</span> + response.error);
    context.fail();
}
</code></pre>
				</div>

<div class="container container-main">

		<div class="col-8 col-content">
			<section class="tsd-panel tsd-comment">
				<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#http" id="http" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>HTTP</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>The <a href="http.html">HTTP</a> and <a href="httpresponse.html">HTTPResponse</a> objects are used to run synchronous HTTP requests to communicate with APIs, or just read pages from the web. A full set of custom settings can be passed, and all HTTP methods (GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, etc.) are supported.</p>
					<a href="#example" id="example" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Example</h3>
					</a>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> http = HTTP.create(); <span class="hljs-comment">// create HTTP object</span>

<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> response = http.request({
  <span class="hljs-string">&quot;url&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;http://myurl.com/api&quot;</span>,
  <span class="hljs-string">&quot;method&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;POST&quot;</span>,
  <span class="hljs-string">&quot;data&quot;</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-string">&quot;key&quot;</span>:<span class="hljs-string">&quot;value&quot;</span>
  },
  <span class="hljs-string">&quot;headers&quot;</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-string">&quot;HeaderName&quot;</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;HeaderValue&quot;</span>
  }
});

<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (response.success) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> text = response.responseText;
  <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> data = response.responseData;
}
<span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
  <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(response.statusCode);
  <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(response.error);
}
</code></pre>
				</div>
			</section>

					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#syntax" id="syntax" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>Syntax</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>Represents a Syntax definition available in the current installation of Drafts.</p>
					<a href="#example-find-and-assign-a-syntax" id="example-find-and-assign-a-syntax" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Example: Find and Assign a Syntax</h3>
					</a>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> syntax = Syntax.find(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;builtIn&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Markdown&quot;</span>);
draft.syntax = syntax;
draft.update();
</code></pre>
				</div>
			</section>

				<div class="tsd-comment tsd-typography">
					<div class="lead">
						<a href="#workspace" id="workspace" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
							<h1>Workspace</h1>
						</a>
					</div>
					<p>Represents a Workspace. Can be used to inquire and load workspaces and apply them using methods on the App object.</p>
					<a href="#example-find-and-load-workspace" id="example-find-and-load-workspace" style="color: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
						<h3>Example: Find and Load Workspace</h3>
					</a>
					<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// find workspace and load it in drafts list</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> workspace = Workspace.find(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Projects&quot;</span>);
app.applyWorkspace(workspace);
</code></pre>
				</div>
			</section>
